         <li id="cite_note-11">
          <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
           <b>
            <a href="#cite_ref-11">
             ^
            </a>
           </b>
          </span>
          <span class="reference-text">
           <cite class="citation" id="CITEREFThompson,_William1891">
            Thompson, William (1891),
            <a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20071224061303/http://www.rongorongo.org/thomson/453.html" rel="nofollow">
             <i>
              Invention of the name 'Rapa Nui'
             </i>
            </a>
            , archived from
            <a class="external text" href="http://www.rongorongo.org/thomson/453.html" rel="nofollow">
             the original
            </a>
            on 24 December 2007
           </cite>
           <span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=Invention+of+the+name+%27Rapa+Nui%27&amp;rft.date=1891&amp;rft.au=Thompson%2C+William&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.rongorongo.org%2Fthomson%2F453.html&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AEaster+Island">
            <span style="display:none;">
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </li>
         <li id="cite_note-12">
          <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
           <b>
            <a href="#cite_ref-12">
             ^
            </a>
           </b>
          </span>
          <span class="reference-text">
           <a href="#CITEREFHeyerdahl1961">
            Heyerdahl 1961
           </a>
           Heyerdahl's view was that the two islands were about the same size, and that "big" and "small" were not physical but historical attributes, "big" indicating the original. In reality, however, Easter Island is more than four times bigger than Rapa Iti. Heyerdahl also stated that there is an island called "Rapa" in
           <a href="/wiki/Lake_Titicaca" title="Lake Titicaca">
            Lake Titicaca
           </a>
           in South America, but so far there is no map available showing an island of that name in the lake.
          </span>
         </li>

           pointed out that the rubble filled Rapanui walls were a fundamentally different design to those of the Inca, as these are trapezoidal in shape as opposed to the perfectly fitted rectangular stones of the Inca. See also

         . Washington: Smithsonian Institution: 447–552.
        </cite>
        <span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft.jtitle=Annual+Reports+of+the+Smithsonian+Institution+for+1889&amp;rft.atitle=Te+Pito+te+Henua%2C+or+Easter+Island.+Report+of+the+United+States+National+Museum+for+the+Year+Ending+June+30%2C+1889&amp;rft.pages=447-552&amp;rft.date=1891&amp;rft.aulast=Thomson&amp;rft.aufirst=William+J.&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AEaster+Island">
         <span style="display:none;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=8gKvwnWvwjsC" rel="nofollow">
         in Google Books
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        <cite class="citation book">
         van Tilburg, Jo Anne (1994).
         <i>
          Easter Island: Archaeology, Ecology and Culture
         </i>
         . Washington, D.C.: Smithsonian Institution Press.
         <a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">
          ISBN
         </a>
         <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0-7141-2504-0" title="Special:BookSources/0-7141-2504-0">
          0-7141-2504-0
         </a>
         .
        </cite>
        <span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=Easter+Island%3A+Archaeology%2C+Ecology+and+Culture&amp;rft.place=Washington%2C+D.C.&amp;rft.pub=Smithsonian+Institution+Press&amp;rft.date=1994&amp;rft.isbn=0-7141-2504-0&amp;rft.aulast=van+Tilburg&amp;rft.aufirst=Jo+Anne&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AEaster+Island">
         <span style="display:none;">
         </span>
        </span>
       </li>
       <li>
        Vergano, Dan.
        <a class="external text" href="https://www.usatoday.com/tech/science/columnist/vergano/2009-11-13-easter-island_N.htm" rel="nofollow">
